voters = JSON.parse(voters);
var v_houses = {}
for(var i=0;i<voters.length;i++){
let v = voters[i];
let h_id=v.fields.house;
if(!v_houses[h_id]){
v_houses[h_id]=[]
v_houses[h_id].push(v)
}else{
v_houses[h_id].push(v)
}
}

function initMap() {
var loaded_map = false;
for(var i=0;i<houses.length;i++){
var p = houses[i];
const position = { lat: parseFloat(p.fields.latitude), lng: parseFloat(p.fields.longitude) };
console.log(p.fields.latitude);
if(!loaded_map){
map = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById("map"), {
center: position,
zoom: 16
});
loaded_map = true;
}
// The marker, positioned at Uluru
const marker = new google.maps.Marker({
position: position,
map: map,
label: ""+(i+1)
});
let voter_str = "";
if(v_houses[p.pk]){
for(var j=0;j<v_houses[p.pk].length;j++){
voter_str+=v_houses[p.pk][j].fields.first_name + " " + v_houses[p.pk][j].fields.last_name + " ("+v_houses[p.pk][j].fields.party.substring(0,1)+")<br/>";
}
}
const infowindow = new google.maps.InfoWindow({
content: "<strong>H#"+(i+1)+":</strong><br/>" +p.fields.address +"<br/><br/>"+voter_str,
});
marker.addListener("click", () => {
if(info_w!=null){
info_w.close();
}
infowindow.open({
anchor: marker,
map,
shouldFocus: false,
});
info_w = infowindow
});
}
}
</script>
</head>

<script

async
></script>
